During interrogation, he denied the charges, saying that he was just passing by and urinating when he saw the letter and picked it up. He was ordered to be detained for further investigation. It was later found that the threatening letter was written by Wu Songquan (15 years old), an apprentice from Wuxi in the store. He was taken into custody at the police station the day before yesterday. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Third Criminal Court with Guo Sen brought to the stand. Zhang Shizhu, a lawyer from the Shanghai Municipal Council, stated that the apprentice Wu had said at the police station that he had written the letter and wanted to switch to being a doctor. He had resigned from Shen's shop on the 14th. Shen then learned about the matter. Under questioning, Wu directly admitted it and was asked to write another letter that was exactly the same. Both letters were submitted for review, and it was requested that Guo Sen be released. The court approved it. When questioned, the apprentice Wu testified, "I want to study medicine, and no one else instructed me to do this." (It was found that the apprentice had been introduced to Xie Changxiang by a relative and had only been there for five days.) His age had not yet passed fourteen. Judge Zhong Qing gave him an admonishment and acquitted Wu Songquan, who was taken back to his hometown by his relative Zhao Guirong to be supervised by his parents.

She Zikang - Rescued After Jumping into the Huangpu River

Four Suicide Notes Detailed Hardship

She Zikang from Yangzhou, 41 years old, was fluent in Chinese and English. He used to work as a scribe at the HSBC Bank in Shanghai and had a good monthly income. Because he was addicted to gambling, She frequented gambling dens every night when they were popular in certain concessions several years ago, spending hundreds of gold coins without hesitation. Eventually, he accumulated huge debts. He even borrowed usurious loans from Indians, who subjected him to constant pressure. After losing his job, he was unable to make a living. His wife also left him to fend for himself. His only son was fostered in his brother-in-law's home. She drifted alone, borrowing from east to west, for the past four or five years. He had no place to eat, and now he had no way to borrow money. He had reached the point of desperation and wanted to end his life. The other day, at dusk, he boarded a Taikoo Company ferry at the Yangjingbang wharf to cross the Huangpu River. When the boat reached the middle of the river, She jumped into the river in an attempt to commit suicide. The captain immediately noticed and stopped the boat, managing to rescue him. He was sent to the Customs Water Police Station, where he explained his situation. Four suicide notes were found on his person. Since he had no family in Shanghai, detectives Huang Songsheng and Fu Guifu were assigned to send him to the Yangzhou Association of Fellow Provincials for relief. The four suicide notes are transcribed below: (1) The suicidee is named She Zikang, 41 years old. He has suffered all kinds of hardships and pain, leading to a lack of mental strength to save himself. Suicide is already six years late. If he had seen fewer unpleasant things six years ago, he would not have lost his family and died now. He feels sorry for himself. (2) To my cousin Deng Xuetai, 5 Xiangshan Lane, Xiangyan Bridge, Shanghai. I asked Jiang Hehe for one and a half yuan the other day, but he completely refused to help. Because of this, I felt ashamed to ask for help in Zhenjiang. Life is destined to end at one hundred years old. What is the pain of dying a few years earlier? My son, Xiao Lin, will have the hardest time. His father is unable to support him and commits suicide. This child will suffer. (3) To Zhu Zheguang and She Yayun, 17 Lane, Chunquan Town Hospital, Lishui, Zhejiang Province. Please treat my son, Yongfang, differently in the future. I was forced to commit suicide by the pressure of life. The mother and son in Ding'an, Hangzhou, will be happy to hear of my suicide. (4) To Hu Atian, Nanyang Lane, Yangshuyuan, Luoshe, Wuxi. Your daughter, Zhao Di, has been avoiding me since I lost my job. She must have other ideas. I have been married to her for thirteen years, like a shadow. Since August 21st of this year, she has been avoiding me, the poor man, and her whereabouts are unknown. Now that I have committed suicide, you and your daughter can be happy. Your daughter doesn't have to avoid me anymore. She can choose another man to live with.

Woman Huang Butian Sues Zhu Ziyun; Zhu Ziyun Case Concluded; Zhu Amao Admits in Court to Being Her Mother; Court Finds Further Confirmation Unnecessary; Settlement Record Created in Court

Huang Butian, the daughter of the late famous national doctor Huang Xiaochu, recently hired lawyer Sha Xunyi to sue national doctor Zhu Ziyun in the First Special District Court, requesting confirmation that Zhu Amao (also known as Yuejuan), the daughter raised by Zhu, was her daughter with Zhu, and to stop Zhu Ziyun from abusing parental rights. Zhu Amao was also listed as the second defendant in the case. The Special Court has summoned the parties several times, but because Zhu Amao had not appeared, the hearing was adjourned. Details of the case have been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Gui Yu continued the hearing of the case in the Seventh Civil Court. The defendant Zhu Ziyun did not appear, but a lawyer appeared on his behalf. Zhu Amao suddenly appeared in court, stating that she was 23 years old, from Jiangwan, and married Zhang Naiwen, who resides at 122, Lane 760, Huishan Road, on October 27 of last year at the Hangzhou Restaurant. She admitted that Huang Butian was her biological mother and that Zhu was her father. She also stated that her father presided over her wedding. The court asked her if Zhu Ziyun admitted that she was his daughter. She replied that he currently did not admit it. The court stated that since Zhu Amao had already admitted it, there was no need for further confirmation, and since Zhu Amao had already married, parental rights had been terminated. Therefore, the court found that the case had no need to be litigated further. Subsequently, Zhu Ziyun's lawyer stated that his client did not admit that Zhu Amao was his daughter at all, and that the case was clearly a conspiracy between the plaintiff and her daughter to target Zhu Ziyun alone. Then, the plaintiff's lawyer requested the court to create a settlement record based on Zhu Amao's admission and to withdraw the part concerning Zhu Ziyun. The court approved the request, and the case was concluded.

China Leprosy Sanatorium; Patients Save on Food to Celebrate Birthday

All patients at the China Leprosy Sanatorium in Dachang celebrated Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's 50th birthday, which fell on the 31st of last month. On that day, they held a birthday commemoration ceremony in the sanatorium's auditorium and also saved one day's worth of vegetable expenses from the patients' food allowance, totaling 12 yuan in national currency, to be used to purchase an airplane. Yesterday, the funds were submitted to the Shanghai Municipal Purchase Airplane Birthday Celebration Committee for receipt so that they could contribute their small share to the effort and fulfill their civic duty. The sanatorium authorities, recognizing the patients' enthusiasm, did not want them to have bland food. Instead, they decided to save the money over a week, with vegetables still being served with meals every day to show their concern. The sanatorium's approach is commendable. It is hoped that other hospitals will follow suit. The money saved would be considerable.

China Merchants Bureau Purchasing Materials; Announcement Strictly Prohibits Swindling

The state-owned China Merchants Bureau purchases materials and ordinary supplies through open bidding by the shipping and general affairs departments, respectively, in accordance with regulations. The winning bids are determined based on the bid price and quality. Recently, the bureau received reports that some people were fabricating facts, boasting, and claiming to have connections, fabricating methods to win bids, and engaging in illegal fraud. The bureau has dispatched personnel for secret investigations and issued a public announcement. In the future, if such incidents occur, once discovered, those involved will not only be subject to administrative penalties but will also be handed over to the court for strict punishment in accordance with the law. Both the givers and receivers will be punished equally, without leniency.

"Minsu" Ship Safely Arrives in Chongqing After Grounding

The "Minsu" ship of the Minsheng Industrial Company ran aground in Shijiatuo on the morning of the 14th. Details were published in yesterday's newspaper. We have received a reliable message from the company that the ship was able to quickly turn its rudder and ran aground on a nearby sandbar, avoiding sinking. At the same time, the ship sent out a distress signal via radio, seeking help from all directions. The passengers were transported to Chongqing by other company vessels, and wooden and more important goods were unloaded onto other ships, minimizing losses. The figures reported in the previous day's newspaper may have been inaccurate rumors. It is also reported that the ship was repaired during low tide with the assistance of the "Minshi" and "Minyong" ships. After the repairs were completed, it was test-driven and, yesterday, the company's Chongqing headquarters telegraphed that the ship had arrived in Chongqing at 5 PM on the 16th. After a brief inspection in Chongqing, it will continue its voyage.

Public Concession Tenders for Cleaning of Excrement Work

The work of cleaning excrement in the Public Concession is contracted out to merchants through bidding every year. The contract for 1936 will expire at the end of this year, so the contract for 1937 is about to be signed. The Public Works Department of the工部局 has issued a tender announcement. Those who wish to bid for the contract should contact the Public Works Department on Hankou Road in accordance with the tender regulations and must deposit 1,000 yuan in national currency at the time of bidding. The deadline for bidding is 11 AM on November 26 of this year.

North Shanghai Station Export Cargo Moved to Maigen Road for Handling

The North Shanghai Station freight yard of the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway has recently experienced an extraordinary amount of cargo congestion, causing the station service office to lack space for storing incoming goods. In order to facilitate the flow of goods, the railway has decided to move the export cargo handling from the North Station service office to the Maigen Road freight station starting on the 16th of this month. Warehouse number 11 at the Maigen Road freight station has been designated for the service office's cargo storage. Telephones will also be installed to facilitate contact with customers.

New China Bank; Small Loan Update

The New China Bank on Jiangxi Road has been providing small credit loans to facilitate the financial needs of professionals for several years. Under the scheme, borrowers must have a legitimate, stable profession, good credit, and find two guarantors to secure the loan. The loan amount per household ranges from 100 to 500 yuan, and is repaid in installments over a maximum of 12 months. Since its inception, the scheme has reportedly made significant progress. Recently, there has been a surge in applications from citizens for legitimate purposes such as weddings, funerals, and education.

Beijing-Shanghai Meiji University Alumni Association Elects Directors and Supervisors

Hu Yizang and Yang Guoshu Elected in Shanghai

After soliciting opinions from various provinces and cities on the merger of the Nanjing Meiji University Alumni Association in Japan to promote emotional connection and facilitate association affairs, all provinces and cities that have established alumni associations have expressed their support. It has been decided to establish a general association in Nanjing and branches in various places. On September 23, an autumn conference was held at 6 Guling Road in Nanjing, and it was decided to add four directors and two supervisors. Election ballots were distributed to alumni in various places, with a deadline of November 10. Yang Yinpu has recently joined the Beijing Alumni Association. Xu Shiying; Representative Arrives in Shanghai to Mourn Duan;

Mrs. Xu Huang Bodu Returned to China by Ship Yesterday Morning

The wife of Xu Shiying, our ambassador to Japan, Mrs. Huang Bodu, along with Huang Bodu, secretary of the Embassy in Japan, arrived in Shanghai at 7 AM yesterday morning aboard the Russian Queen of the Changxing Shipping Company. After disembarking at the Gonghexiang Wharf, they returned to their private residences to rest. Mrs. Xu, fatigued from the sea voyage, planned to visit the Duan residence on Avenue Joffre this morning to offer condolences. Huang Bodu visited the residence yesterday morning at 11 AM to offer condolences. Ambassador Xu, upon learning of Duan Qirui's death, originally intended to return to the country to offer condolences in person, but his leave request was not approved. Therefore, he sent his wife back to the country to represent him in offering condolences. He plans to return to the country when Duan's state funeral is held. Mrs. Xu carried many handwritten letters from Xu to important figures in Beijing and Shanghai, a portion of which was delivered by Huang Bodu yesterday morning. Mrs. Xu, having not returned to the country for a long time, plans to stay in Shanghai for an extended period and will return to Japan with Ambassador Xu after he returns to the country. Huang plans to stay in the country for two or three weeks and will take the night train to Beijing tonight to meet with Foreign Minister Zhang and report on the situation. Xu Shiying's eulogy for Duan is recorded as follows: "一生剛介·三造共和·定大難·决大疑·峙如泰山·渟如止水·晚節愈堅貞·莽莽乾坤能有幾、卅載論交·百年知己·言可坊·行可表·進思盡忠·退思補過·衷腸今割裂、茫茫人海更何之、" (A life of integrity, three times creating the Republic, resolving great difficulties and doubts, standing like Mount Tai, as still as stagnant water, his integrity growing stronger in his later years, how many are there like this in this vast universe? Thirty years of friendship, a century of knowing each other, his words are exemplary, his actions are a model, in advancement thinking of loyalty, in retirement thinking of making amends, my heart is now torn, where in this vast sea of humanity can I find another like him?)

Waiter Training School; Truth About the Current Recruitment

In order to clarify the waiter training school recruitment advertisement, the details are as follows: The organizers of the school are Mr. Lu and others, formerly of the International Hotel Waiter Training School. Mr. Lu felt that the waiters serving at the International Hotel were indeed superior to those who had not been trained. Their demeanor, speech, and manners were free of vulgarity and were not offensive to customers. Therefore, he believed that training was not only necessary for the hotel industry but also for other professions, as it could greatly benefit management in all aspects. Recently, due to the flourishing business of the International Hotel, the original number of waiters was insufficient, prompting the current recruitment and training. As there were also commissions from other hotels to train waiters, the future demand would not be limited to the International Hotel alone. Therefore, it was decided not to use the International Hotel name. Fearing that too many unqualified applicants would apply, the application fee was increased to five yuan to limit the number of applicants, but this fee would be deducted from the tuition fee in the future. The tuition fee of 100 yuan reportedly includes room, board, medical expenses, and other fees, so it cannot be considered high. Furthermore, the school strives to provide the best possible facilities to cultivate good habits in the waiters and eliminate all traces of simplicity. The training period is only three months. During these three months, the school focuses on character, then physical fitness, and finally knowledge. With good character and a healthy body, it is easier to make progress in knowledge. The test results will be used to determine future service performance. Those with excellent character and potential will be sent to commissioned organizations for practical training. Those with poor character and untrainable will be eliminated. It is also reported that Mr. Lu and others conducted another experiment, which yielded excellent results. They plan to continue training workers in various industries to cultivate talent, provide legitimate employment opportunities for the unemployed, and lay the foundation for the advancement of social enterprises. This is a great initiative for social vocational education in the city. The school's first recruitment was held on the 15th of this month. It is reported that few candidates passed. The school plans to continue recruiting more candidates, with classes scheduled to begin in early December. The school is located at 5511 Zhongshan Road, the former dormitory for waiters at the International Hotel. It is also reported that the school has officially registered with the municipal authorities to avoid misunderstandings among those who are unaware of the facts.

Bangzi Opera First Time in the South; Central Theater to Perform Starting Today

Bangzi opera has been popular in North China for a long time, with many famous actors. In the South, it was only occasionally seen in Peking opera troupes in the past, and it has become a thing of the past in recent years. The Central Grand Theater has recently hired male and female performers from the Hebei Yisu Bangzi Opera Troupe, such as Ge Wenjuan, Xiao Yuying, Xiao Yulan, Xiao Wuduo, Wang Jufen, and more than 60 others, all of whom are outstanding talents famous in Tianjin and Beijing. It is scheduled to start today, with two performances every day, performing their signature masterpieces to satisfy the people of Shanghai. This is the first time that an entire Bangzi opera troupe has come to the South. It is expected that the revival of ancient tunes will be refreshing and will be extremely popular.

Great Legal Scholar Zhang Shituan Passes Away

Great legal scholar and famous lawyer Zhang Shituan (Qi Han) passed away at 8 AM on the 16th at his residence at 149 Shiquan Street in Suzhou. The funeral is scheduled for the 18th. Zhang was a veteran of the legal profession. He studied in Japan during the late Qing Dynasty and was a Juren in the legal and political examinations of the Xuantong reign. He served as the director and chief prosecutor of various local courts, the chief prosecutor of the Jiangsu High Court, and a prosecutor in the General Prosecutor's Office. He joined the Shanghai, Wuxian, and Jiangning Bar Associations successively and practiced law. He was currently the vice president of the Wuxian Bar Association and a standing committee member of the National Bar Association. Zhang devoted himself to the revolution for 20 years. He joined the Tongmenghui in Japan in 1906. After the founding of the Republic, he reorganized the Kuomintang and served as a councilor of the Jiangsu Party Department and a standing committee member of the Wuxian District Party Department. He also served as a law professor at various universities for more than 20 years, and his students, numbering no less than 10,000, are all serving in the judicial field. Zhang was generally healthy but suffered from liver and stomach ailments in recent years, which led to his decline. His passing is deeply mourned by his colleagues in the legal profession.

Zhou Lihua's Art Exhibition Day Two

Yesterday was the second day of female painter Zhou Lihua's solo Western painting exhibition. Visitors included Xu Langxi, president of the Xinhua Art College, Secretary Geng of the Municipal Government, famous photographer Lu Shifu, and Hu Shuyi of the Xinwen Daily. Several paintings were successively reserved, including "April in the Countryside, Few People" reserved by Mr. Xu and "Report" and "Skylight and Cloud Shadow" reserved by Mr. Lu Peizhi. The Jiangning Guildhall at the intersection of Xinzha Road and Chengdu Road was accused, requesting the Municipal Party Department to send personnel to reorganize it. Huang Chunquan, Tu Xiaochao, Zhang Huachen, and Weng Hongbin resigned after being appointed, and the Municipal Party Department approved their resignations and designated the remaining five, Dai Zhifu, and others, as reorganization committee members, with Lu Yinchu as the advisor and Dai Zhifu as the convener of the first meeting. (3) All staff members originally employed at the Guildhall will continue to work as usual. (4) Send a letter to former executive director Huang Chunquan to handle the handover. New Contributions of the New Asia Pharmaceutical Factory

The Star Brand medicines produced by the Shanghai New Asia Pharmaceutical Factory, numbering over several hundred varieties, all possess considerable efficacy and reputation. Among them, the "Fu Bai Long" injection for treating malaria and reducing fever has long been adopted by physicians. "Danggui Er" liquid, a gynecological medicine for regulating menstruation, specifically treats irregular menstruation, painful menstruation, and amenorrhea in women, demonstrating the most remarkable effectiveness, with sales already covering the entire country and reaching the South Seas Islands. It is now heard that, in order to make it more convenient to take, the factory has added sugar-coated tablets of the above two medicines. The medicinal strength and function remain unchanged. These are now being sold on the market, and major pharmacies all have them for sale.

Fire at the Intersection of Avenue Edward VII and Guangxi Road – Yong An Lane Fire Last Night

At 11:30 last night, a sudden mishap occurred at No. 9 Yong An Lane, at the intersection of Avenue Edward VII and Guangxi Road. Thick smoke spread everywhere, and the fire was extremely fierce. It immediately spread to Nos. 7, 5, and 11. The fire brigade rushed to the scene and tried their best to put out the fire, which was extinguished after about two hours. As a result, Nos. 9 and 7 were completely destroyed, and a corner of the roof of Nos. 5 and 11 were also burned.

Letter

To the Editor,

Having read your newspaper yesterday, the news column of this city included a report about Da Guangming and other theaters refusing to show films celebrating birthdays, and also included the name of our theater among them. Upon investigation, our theater has been extremely enthusiastic in supporting the donation of airplanes for birthdays, and on Generalissimo Chiang's birthday, we showed Generalissimo Chiang's likeness, various slogans, and films celebrating the birthday, etc. Receipts for both the donation and showing are kept on file. Thus, what is written in your newspaper obviously does not conform to the facts. In order to avoid misunderstanding, please correct this.

Sincerely,

Shanghai Grand Theatre

The Xujiahui Observatory issued a weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday, stating that the Shandong area is cloudy with unstable conditions, with southwest to northwest winds. The Yellow River basin has sand and northwest winds. The upper and middle reaches of the Yangtze River have rain and northeast winds. The lower reaches of the Yangtze River are cloudy and gradually changing, with fog and winds from the southeast to northeast, due to a low pressure in the southern tide. The East China Sea and Taiwan are cloudy with strong northeast winds. General Overview of the Fluctuations in Shanghai's Industry and Commerce in July and August of This Year (Continued) (No. 38 of the Overview of Shanghai's Industry and Commerce)

— Compiled by China Credit Bureau

3. The Opening of the Chinese and Western Cuisine Department of the Daxin Restaurant - The restaurant is located on the fifth floor of the Daxin Company and is operated by the Daxin Ballroom under contract from the Daxin Company. The ballroom then leased the Chinese cuisine department to Mr. Wang Weibiao, who serves as the general manager of the Chinese cuisine department, and Mr. Su Zhangyu is hired as the manager. All the equipment for the department is owned by the Daxin Ballroom. The department opened on the 28th, simultaneously with the Western cuisine department.

The following four major changes in the manufacturing industry in August can be listed:

1. The Opening of the Tongfeng Printing and Dyeing Company - The company was reorganized from the Jingfeng Printing and Dyeing Factory and the Hongfeng Printing and Dyeing Company. After the Jingfeng Printing and Dyeing Factory declared its closure due to business losses, Mr. Han Chongqin and others raised funds to set up the Hongfeng Printing and Dyeing Company and rented all the machinery of the factory from the Jingfeng creditors. However, the conditions were not appropriate and were opposed by the shareholders and some of the creditors of the factory, so the deal did not materialize. Later this month, Mr. Han and others reached an agreement with both parties and signed a lease agreement, changing the original name of Hongfeng to Tongfeng. The paid-up capital is 60,000 yuan, and it is organized as a joint-stock company. Shareholder Han Changsheng is elected as the chairman of the board, and Han Chongqin is the manager. The company specializes in purchasing raw cloth for printing, dyeing, and sales. 2. The Opening of the Yuanyuan Xingji Milk Company - The company was transformed from the former Yuanyuan Farm. Since the farm was unable to repay its debts due to poor business performance, it was sealed up by the Jincheng Bank and was forced to liquidate in October of last year. All of its assets were auctioned off by the court. Mr. Hao Duoshi purchased it from the court, unsealed it, and changed its name to Yuanyuan Xingji Milk Company. The company is a joint-stock company and hired Mr. Cao Bentao to oversee everything. The company is quite large and well-equipped, with total assets worth 500,000 to 600,000 yuan.

Yesterday, the gold market continued to decline in pure gold, and people's hearts were slightly tired. Securities - Why are Public Bonds Being Sold Off in a Rush?

Yesterday at the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange, the market continued to decline. The long positions of major traders exited the market, showing signs of rushing to sell. Judging from its background, the Suiyuan War may expand. The bond market is trending downward, mostly due to the exit of long positions. The outflow of spot bonds is also considerable. Yarn and Cotton - Floating Long Positions Take Profits – The Yarn Market Reverses – Major Traders Are Still Importing in This Month

After rising for a day, the yarn market showed signs of a reversal and decline again yesterday. This was because the price was too high, customers' yarn sales were sluggish, and people's hearts were hit by the intense Suiyuan War. Floating long positions took profits, and the market reversed. However, major traders were still importing, and the rise in Osaka Sanpin yarn revived.

The Standard Yarn Market Enters a Weak Path

At the opening of the standard yarn market, the trend was flat and weak due to the intense Suiyuan War and the decline in Osaka Sanpin yarn. After the second session, floating long positions exited the market, and the market price declined step by step. However, long positions continued to tighten and refused to let go, absorbing a huge amount. However, the sales of spot yarn were quite sluggish, and people's hearts were weak. As a result, the standard yarn market fell by 1.30 yuan to 1.90 yuan in each month compared to the closing price of the previous day. At the afternoon closing, the Osaka Sanpin yarn still rose, and the sentiment was strong, rebounding by several tenths of a cent. Then, as yarn transactions became sluggish and the price of Jincheng yarn fell, the market entered a weak path again. As a result, this month rose by 1.10 yuan compared to the closing price of the previous day, and the far month rose by 30 to 40 cents. The sellers were Gengfeng, Zhanmai, and Ma, while the buyers were Xiecheng (1,300 bales), Dachangcheng (1,200 bales), Dafeng (900 bales), Yukang (800 bales), Hexing (3,550 bales), Gengfeng (2,900 bales), Changji (1,200 bales), Hengde (1,050 bales), Dachang (3,550 bales), and Fengtai (1,200 bales). The buyers were Hengyi (2,400 bales), Yuda (1,400 bales), Jinchang (2,550 bales), Mingde (1,700 bales), Renfeng (950 bales), Taichang (1,400 bales), Yichang (3,750 bales), Changfeng (7,400 bales), Fengtaixing (1,100 bales), and Yongda (900 bales). The highest and lowest prices for the day are listed on the left.

Cotton Slightly Turns Soft

The cotton market is calm, but overseas American cotton has rebounded. Although the cotton production estimate has been reduced by 2 million piculs, it is still outside of 14 million piculs, so people's hearts are still ordinary. However, the need for cotton mills is developing, and both domestic and foreign factories are actively purchasing.

The Standard Cotton Market Steps Down by 30 to 40 Cents

At the opening of the standard cotton market in the morning, the prices for each month varied, rising or falling by 5 cents to 15 cents. Then, as the published estimate for this year's cotton production was reduced by 2 million piculs, but still outside of 14 million piculs, people's hearts were ordinary, and the selling pressure increased slightly. At the same time, the yarn market was weak. As a result, each month fell by 25 cents to 30 to 40 cents compared to the closing price of the previous day. The opening in the afternoon was flat. Discussions in the market stated that Russian cotton production reportedly accounts for the third largest in the world, and most people were bearish on this. This amount is feared to be incorrect, and it is said to be the amount of seed cotton. However, although the world's cotton production is celebrating a bumper harvest, the American cotton futures are still firm and expensive. The closing remained normal. As a result, each month was similar to the previous day. The sellers were Hexing (5,800 piculs), Xincheng (2,800 piculs), Ruida (2,600 piculs), Meiji (3,800 piculs), Yongyu (2,300 piculs), Changyu (8,000 piculs), Fengtai (3,100 piculs), Renfeng (4,400 piculs), Dachangcheng (1,500 piculs), and Xiecheng (1,900 piculs). General Overview of the Second Estimate of National Cotton Production - Cotton Fields Increase, Cotton Production Decreases - But 6 Million More Than Last Year

The China Cotton Industry Statistics Association announced the second estimate of national cotton production for 1936 at 5:00 PM on November 16th as follows:

Cotton Field Area 345,862.422 "hectares"

Total 51,879,000 "Chinese mu"

Total 56,292,711 "Old System Mu"

Lint Production 8,468,644 "Metric Piculs"

Total 16,937.000 "Chinese Piculs"

Total 14,429,291 "Old System Piculs"

Wasted Field Area 543,130 "Hectares"

Total 81,000 "Chinese mu"

Total 88,400 "Old System Mu"

This estimate (1) is based on reports from 12 provinces, including Hebei, Shandong, Shanxi, Henan, Shaanxi, Hubei, Hunan, Jiangxi, Anhui, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Sichuan, and the two cities of Shanghai and Tianjin, (2) is based on the cotton crop situation before November 10th, (3) The losses suffered by the cotton crops in various provinces before November 10th have been included in the calculation, (4) Each mu of cotton field in the "Old System Mu" is 60 square zhang in the Ministry of Works measurement, and each picul of cotton production in the "Old System Picul" is 100 jin on the Tianping scale.

A comparison of the cotton field production estimates of the Association over the years is shown below (the terms "hectares", "Chinese mu", "metric piculs", and "Chinese piculs" are not indicated in the table and text, all of which are "Old System Mu" and "Old System Picul")

The national cotton production situation was generally good this year. From the initial sowing stage to the time of the Association's first estimate, the climate was extremely suitable in both the Yangtze River cotton region and the Yellow River cotton region. Therefore, on the one hand, the cotton field area increased greatly, and on the other hand, the harvest was good. Therefore, the first estimate of the national production reached more than 16,379,000 piculs, with an average yield of almost 30 jin per mu, which is a rare bumper harvest in recent years. After the first estimate, the situation was still good at first. In the Yellow River basin, the timely rainfall was suitable, and the cotton plants developed well. In the Yangtze River region, only the salt reclamation area of Jiangsu suffered from rain and water disasters, but most of the region did not have the autumn wind and rain, and the sunny and warm weather was especially helpful for the growth of late flowers and late bolls. The cotton harvest still had the potential to continue to improve. Unexpectedly, this sunny and warm climate continued to extend for almost two months without rain. The cotton crops initially suffered from drought and eventually declared disaster. The national cotton region was almost the same. The typhoons in Jiangsu and Zhejiang were rare, which was greatly beneficial to the harvest, but the losses from the drought were probably not small. However, because Zhejiang received rain, it still made progress, and most of the rest of the regions reported reduced production. Due to the different severity of the drought, the reduction rates were slightly different. Sichuan Province was hit by both water and drought disasters in succession, and suffered particularly heavy losses. It is estimated that the national cotton field area is 96,292,712 mu, an increase of 1,251,646 mu compared to the first estimate, and the production is 14,439,291 piculs, a decrease of 1,939,903 piculs compared to the first estimate, but still an increase of 6,296,380 piculs compared to 1935. The average yield per mu is about 26 jin, a decrease of more than 3 jin compared to the first estimate, and an increase of more than 2 jin compared to the actual harvest last year, which is still the highest harvest in the last five years.

American Cotton Shows a Firm and Rising Trend

Yesterday, American cotton opened with a drop of 3 pounds to a rise of 1 pound. Most of the trading in the market was for long positions to take profits and hedge sales, and December terms were transferred to the far term. There were not many over-the-counter transactions, and both sides were evenly matched. The spot cotton prices were firm, and the cloth market was relatively sluggish. The American cotton situation was firm and rising. However, world cotton production increased. Although there was frost in the east, it was generally believed that the cotton harvest was over, which was insignificant. Later, the stock market and other commodity prices rose, and the industry actively bought in, pushing up the market price. Spot prices rose by 11 pounds, and futures prices rose by 11 to 15 pounds. Spot prices for British cotton fell by 3 points, and futures prices fell by 2 or 3 points. Indian cotton was initially firm due to purchases by European exporters, but later weakened due to sales by speculators, long position profit-taking, and unfavorable news from Liverpool. Phergal fell by 0.5 to 0.75 rupees, Omra fell by 1.5 to 2.5 rupees, and Bai Luo Creek fell by 2 rupees. The original telegram is recorded on the left (telegram dated 16th).

Phergal 157.50 down 0.75 27.80

March Term 158.00 0.40 17.90

Omra 196.00 2.50 34.80

March Term 194.75 1.50 34.60

Bai Luo Creek 215.25 2.00 38.20

According to a telegram from Bombay, the opening forecast for the 17th was Bai Luo Creek at 217.5 rupees, up 2.25 rupees, Omra at 198 rupees, up 2 rupees, and Phergal at 159 rupees, up 1.9 rupees.

Last Week's Cotton Exports from Rangoon

According to a telegram from Bombay on the 16th, the amount of cotton exported by buyers in Rangoon last week totaled 539 tons, of which 325 tons were to Kobe, 8 tons to Mawei, 71 tons to Osaka, and 54 tons to Nagasaki.

Sanpin Yarn and Cotton Rise Quite Sharply

According to a telegram from Osaka on the 17th, the three types of yarn futures rose by 1.90 yuan to 3.20 yuan, with the near month at 238 yuan and the far month at 212.80 yuan. Cotton futures rose by 40 cents to 95 cents, with the near month at 65.95 yuan and the far month at 66.79 yuan.

Silk and Tea: The Flourishing Silk Market Will Soon Come to an End

Yesterday, the overseas silk market clearly showed signs of a downturn. Trading on the New York Stock Exchange saw general declines. Day silk was averaging 83 and 75, Shanghai silk and Guangdong silk each fell by one point, far-term standard silk futures dropped by three and a half points, and near-term futures fell by as much as five points. Converted to Shanghai prices, each dan (unit of weight) of raw silk fell by over twenty yuan. Yokohama silk prices also saw a slight correction, with spot prices down two yuan and futures down twelve yuan. The Lyon silk market, however, was relatively firm, with Japanese silk and Shanghai silk of the B grade rising slightly, and the rest remaining at their original prices. The Shanghai silk market is currently experiencing a slowdown in foreign sales due to the low prices abroad and excessively harsh price limits. The silk market, which has been flourishing for over a month, may now be coming to an end. Domestic silk sales were also very sparse yesterday, but fortunately, trading prices remained unchanged. A total of sixty bales of white filature and other silks were sold throughout the day.

Shenbao National Products Special

Words of Contribution

Textiles: Cotton Cloth Demand is Strongest in Sichuan and Yunnan

Yesterday, the cotton cloth market continued to be strong. Domestic yarn and cotton prices were stable, and top-grade American cotton all showed increases. Market sentiment was extremely robust, and the prices of various goods for sale were all very firm. Actual sales gradually developed, with the Southwest regions being the best. Yesterday, merchants from Sichuan and Yunnan continued to purchase over 300 pieces of goods, including in-color goods, printed velvet, khaki drill, sheeting, linen cloth, serge, twill, white fine cloth, and coarse cloth. However, goods from Fujian Province saw little activity. Previously ordered low-priced goods were gradually being delivered, but shipments were not surging. Some goods have already been resold in Shanghai, likely because the markets in Guangdong and Fujian Provinces are difficult to turn around. Actual demand in Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and Anhui Provinces continues to be strong. Sales in Zhejiang Province, including Ningbo, Shaoxing, Jinhua, Hengyan, and other places, are recovering, but Quzhou and Taizhou remain stagnant. Merchants from Shaanxi and Henan Provinces are gradually seeing opportunities, with most purchases being serge, straight tribute cloth, linen cloth, and white flannel. White goods from Tianjin merchants remain stagnant. Yesterday, there were quite a few purchases of colored goods, with transactions including eighty bolts of Junzi serge and over thirty cases of linen cloth from various Chinese factories. The most active business on this street is still flannel.

Grain: Actual Sales are Stagnant, Fluctuations in Futures of Flour and Wheat are Very Small

Flour: Yesterday, after the market opened in the morning, prices for all months initially seemed stable. Due to the quotations for foreign wheat, with Chicago rising about 3 to 4 cents and Canada rising 1.0 cent, the opening prices caused a slight tremor in market sentiment. Near-term months were slightly better, while far-term months were slightly better by 1 to 2 cents. However, local factories, due to sluggish actual sales, were expected to sell off far-term contracts, causing the market to soften again. The situation for this month to March was similar to the previous day, while April saw a slight decrease of 0.5 cent. By the afternoon opening, trading became quiet, and prices for all months tended to be stagnant. Speculation was difficult to exploit, and grain prices in various regions were also stagnant. Buyers are naturally adopting a wait-and-see approach. Unless there are special changes, it is expected that prices will fluctuate within a narrow range.

Wheat: Yesterday, the wheat futures market saw very little fluctuation in prices for various months in the morning. Although foreign wheat continued to perform well, due to the scarcity of buyers and the cautious approach of sellers, both sides were reluctant to engage, leading to quiet trading. Although foreign wheat prices were not favorable, compared to domestic rice prices, wheat prices were already on par. Looking back at the facts, this caused buyers to hesitate. By the afternoon opening, trading remained slow. Near-term months were slightly softer, while far-term months were stable. Looking ahead, it is feared that prices will fluctuate for a while. The wheat market remains calm, with very little fluctuation. High-quality wheat from Wuhe Yaowan opened at 8.05 yuan, Shaoxing wheat at 5.93 yuan, and Nanjing Dongtai wheat from the whole city at 5.85 yuan, with a total of over 10,000 bags offered.

Soybeans are Entirely Controlled by Dalian

Recently, the soybean market situation has been entirely manipulated by Dalian. The speed of fluctuations in the Dalian market from day to day is so rapid that the market's atmosphere makes it impossible for buying and selling to respond to each other. This causes procurement to be hesitant, with only sporadic inquiries. Total transactions in the market are less than 1,000 bags, and oil extraction plants are unwilling to pay high prices. The future trend is unlikely to be prosperous.

Observations of National Products and Nanyang Commerce Delegation

— Yang An

The position of national products in Nanyang has been declining in recent years, almost without the prosperity of the past. This is because the domestic industrial sector has not paid attention to it, while Europe, America, and Japan, relying on their superior forces, have encroached and seized market share, and their influence has grown. Nanyang and national products can no longer be a combined term.

In July of this year, the China National Industries Foreign Trade Association organized the Nanyang Business Observation Delegation. With products from 37 factories, under the leadership of Director Gao and Hu, they went to various places in Nanyang, such as the Philippines, Singapore, Batavia, Penang, Medan, Surabaya, Siam, and Saigon, for a period of four months, covering a distance of over ten thousand miles. They returned to the country yesterday, with great success and reputation. All sectors warmly welcomed them to commend all members of the delegation at sea, which was a grand event. The five members believe that the Nanyang Business Observation Delegation gained a lot. The most outstanding ones are as follows:

(1) To show people the true picture of national products, so that compatriots understand the progress of national products over the years, which is indeed not to be underestimated, and to evoke the enthusiasm of Nanyang compatriots to use national products. It is reported that the National Products Exhibition held has more than 10,000 visitors every day, leaving a very good impression on the people of Nanyang.

(2) The power of this visit is the greatest for the emotional connection between domestic manufacturers and Nanyang compatriots. Not only does it connect the feelings of compatriots, but also the feelings between governments in various places have become connected, eliminating the past drawbacks of isolation. This time, the entire delegation received grand receptions and welcomes from local governments and local Chinese merchants wherever they went. This has never happened before, and the gentlemen of the Observation Delegation have successfully achieved their effect.

(3) To gain the trust of compatriots in the motherland. Compatriots see that the products of the motherland are so excellent, and the leaders of the industrial sector have such talent, and a passion arises spontaneously, leading to purchases and orders, and they are willing to act as distributors, and even want to set up China National Products Companies and introduction offices, to cooperate sincerely with domestic partners. This kind of loving and sincere attitude is unprecedented since the beginning of Nanyang trade, and it is also a credit to the gentlemen of the Observation Delegation.

Based on these three points, we respectfully predict with twelve points of enthusiasm that the future of national products in Nanyang has unlimited prospects.

Two Valuable Suggestions in the Midst of the National Products Movement

— Interviewer — Xu Songzi

"Selecting and hiring female interviewers to go to homes for conversations, to discuss with housewives the common knowledge of identifying national products, and to inquire about the criticisms of various housewives regarding various national products, so as to inform manufacturers to improve."

This is the purpose of the interviews issued by our association - the Shanghai National Products Movement Federation before dispatching us to homes.

Now, the home visit work has begun for two weeks. Although we have to encounter many hard and soft nails every day, sometimes we use all kinds of methods and cannot open the door of the housewife; although due to the economic downturn and the "imbalance of education level," we will everywhere be obstructed by bad ideas such as "the fundraisers are here again," "it must be a female swindler," "the pushy salesmen are here," etc. In fact, we have broken through many difficulties. Our work can not be said to be advancing under relatively smooth conditions.

Our work is arduous, but we have gained supreme joy and supreme reward in our work!

What is the reward we get? It is the emotional hospitality of the general housewives, the resonance of our hearts. Listen, are they not saying:

"We are all Chinese, and Chinese blood flows in our veins. National crisis cannot be said to have reached the endpoint, and buying foreign goods is such a cruel and unreasonable thing!"

Not only that, but more worth remembering are the housewives' suggestions for the National Products Movement. Yes, according to the purpose of the interview, the faithful opinions of the housewives are worth sincerely accepting and improving. Only in this way can the National Products Movement progress and the National Products market have the possibility of leaping forward. Combining their conversations, we can offer the following two valuable suggestions.

1. Establish a National Products Consultation Center.

Establishing a National Products Consultation Center is a major issue, but the reason is very simple. Because home visits are only short-term work, the maximum effect is only to give housewives a good impression for a short time. In order to maintain the power of the visit work permanently, we can only establish National Products Consultation Centers in the central locations of various districts in this city, so that housewives in each district can come to consult nearby. Because everyone knows that they should love and use national products, but there are some unscrupulous merchants who have lost their conscience and are greedy for short-term profits, and often use foreign goods to counterfeit national products, so that people who buy national products cannot distinguish the authenticity, and often go to buy goods happily, but after careful examination, the result is a fake foreign product, or even inferior goods. At this time, a piece of enthusiasm is exchanged for a stomach full of sadness! Therefore, the establishment of National Products Consultation Centers in various districts can not only provide consultation for housewives, but also promote new national products in a timely manner for housewives to use. Therefore, it is a very important work.

2. The Necessity of Establishing National Products Companies in Various Districts.

Indeed, we already have large-scale National Products Companies, which are sufficient for patriots to choose and buy national products. However, daily necessities are mostly added to the family temporarily. It is not very reliable to seek them in general stores. If you go to Nanjing Road and other places to buy them, it is inevitable that it will be inconvenient and costly. If obvious National Products Companies can be established in various districts, even on larger roads (the size does not matter), so that the general housewives can clearly know that they are national products, and because of the convenience, they will inevitably buy from National Products Companies, there is no doubt.

The above suggestions can only be said to be very general opinions, as for the specific methods, they need to be developed and supported by the advanced members of the National Products community and the ladies and gentlemen of the society!

The Four "Musts" for Promoting National Products

— Zhang Zhang

Promoting national products is the unanimous cry of all enlightened people in the country in recent years. However, in my opinion, the reason why the achievements in promoting national products have not been 120% significant is that the general compatriots have not been able to practice the four "must" principles. What are the four "must" principles? Please see below:

(1) Must Gladly Use National Products: It is a matter of course and an undeniable fact that Chinese people should use Chinese goods. We should have an attitude of being happy to buy and use national products. Whether it is the smallest needle or the consumption of a piece of paper, whenever national products are available, we should always give priority to buying and using national products. If everyone has this spirit of being happy to use national products, the future of the national products industry will naturally develop rapidly and reach a successful state.

(2) Must Forgive National Products: Some people say: "It's not that I don't want to use Chinese goods, but in reality, compared to non-national products, there is a difference in substance. For the sake of durability, I have to reluctantly buy foreign goods. It's not that I'm happy to use foreign goods, it's really a last resort." People with this attitude are probably not a small number in today's society. I think we should have an attitude of forgiving national products. Although there may be a difference in substance compared to other products, we should still be happy to buy and use them because these are our Chinese national products, and forgive them. With this spirit of forgiving national products, foreign goods will fundamentally not be able to be dumped in large quantities in the Chinese market, and China's economic crisis will naturally have a day of salvation.

(3) Must Urge National Products: Promoting national products should not only be about consumption, and should also try to use them as much as possible, but also actively improve the production sector in order to reach perfection. For general national products that we think need to be improved, we should sincerely offer suggestions to the national products production sector, urging them to find ways to improve. If we can do this, the substance of national products will have the possibility of progress and will be happily used by consumers.

(4) Must Recognize National Products: Finally, let's talk about the issue of recognizing national products. Currently, there are many people who mistakenly purchase foreign goods and counterfeit goods because they do not recognize national products. This is something that should be remedied. Therefore, we should go to national products exhibitions as much as possible to increase our knowledge and ability to identify national products. For example, the National Exhibition organized by the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce is currently in progress, and it is well worth a visit for compatriots who do not know much about national products.

Brief News: Since the pseudo-Mongolian bandit army attacked Suiyuan Province, the situation in the northern border has suddenly become tense. It is now reported that General Fu Zuoyi is directing the battle. However, the soldiers on the front line are serving the country in this icy and snowy environment, and their supplies are in urgent need of assistance from the rear. The owner of the Zhengtai Rubber Factory in this city, in view of this situation, in addition to gathering all the employees of the factory to donate a large sum of money, which was remitted to the front line through this newspaper, also donated 2,000 pairs of Warrior athletic shoes, which were also transferred by this newspaper. It is hoped that major companies and factories will follow suit, and the soldiers fighting on the front line will feel grateful.

Spring and Autumn

Tidbits

— (Fan Xianwei)

There are two kinds of faces in the world that are the most difficult to look at, except for the dying patient on the sickbed and the blood of the death row inmate waiting to be shot on the execution ground: one is the face of a wealthy person who is puffing out their chest and belly, the face of a person who gains property and a debt collector - the other is the face of a poor person who is hunching over and stooping - the face of an unemployed person and a person who is borrowing money. The former's every word and deed reveals an arrogant attitude, and it is necessary to take advantage of everything in every way, making people angry - the latter is absolutely the opposite, revealing a cramped and uneasy state everywhere, with flattering smiles, doing everything possible, with the feeling of "suffering a loss now is a small matter, I only hope that the other party will be lenient", making people feel disgusted when they see it!

Opportunity is like the wind in the sky, and people are like the sails on a ship. If there is wind but no sails are raised, you are giving up your rights. If there are sails but no wind, there is naturally no way. This all depends on the captain's own discretion. However, even if the wind is good, the most common mistake is to have the sails set too full. It's better to give up one or two points! That way it will be fast and stable, otherwise, if a gust of wind hits, the mast will break and the boat will capsize, which is not good. If you ask where the opportunity is? You don't have to look far, it's worthless, it's just the four words "seize the reality"!

"Picking Up Fallen Cotton"

— Wo Fo

The story of "Daiyu Burying Flowers" in "Dream of the Red Chamber" has been passed down as a beautiful story by later generations. Other things like "counting fallen flowers," "sweeping fallen flowers," and "chanting fallen flowers" are all the leisure and elegance of noble hermits, worthy of people's envy. But the "picking up fallen cotton" mentioned here, the flowers are not the kind of peony, peony, hibiscus and other flowers that are only for people to admire, and their picking up fallen cotton is definitely not the leisure and elegance used by noble hermits to pass the time, but comes from the drive of hunger and cold. It turns out that the flowers are cotton, and those who are engaged in picking up fallen cotton are those hungry people who have no way to maintain their lives!

It's that time again, and the scene of picking up fallen cotton reappears in my mind after meeting someone from my hometown. Originally, the farmers in the countryside, of course, collect the cotton in their fields very carefully, but no matter how careful they are, they will inevitably leave some remnants or late-blooming cotton there, and the farmers are not willing to spend any more effort to pick them up. Therefore, at that time, the general poor people in the countryside usually sent out all the men and women of the family to engage in the work of picking up fallen cotton (also called "picking up fallen flowers"): they used their sharp eyes, meticulous observation, agile wrists, and quick steps to pick up the fallen flowers that are not easily seen by ordinary people, that have been eaten by insects or attached to dry leaves. In this way, the fallen flowers they pick up all day, when plentiful, can also get three or five pounds: then they add a procedure of removing dirt and sorting the fallen flowers picked up by the family during this period, and take the better ones to the market to exchange for money and rice, and the damaged ones are made into cotton wool for warmth. In this way, they have solved part of their hunger and cold problems, so they often say to people: "We are not picking up fallen cotton, we are saving our lives." Fortunately, in the past, the landlords did not interfere very much with this kind of behavior.

But in recent years, it has been different. The landlords themselves are also threatened by hunger and cold. How can they be willing to let people pick up all their fallen cotton? So, on the one hand, they prohibit those who pick up fallen cotton from entering their fields, and on the other hand, they do the work of picking up fallen cotton themselves. Therefore, the poor people in the countryside now have no way to save their lives - fallen cotton. Alas!

Ivory Soap

— Junmei

My neighbor, Mr. Chen, lost his elegant seal script and given name many years ago, and is always called "Ivory Soap". Mr. Chen himself admits that this respected name is true to its name. Before the restoration, he had served as a patrol inspector, and after the restoration, he had also held the title of some kind of councilor. Therefore, he is not a first-class country gentleman here, but at least he is a respectable Mr. Official. The thing that he usually thinks is painful and often puts on his lips is that during his tenure as a patrol inspector, he spent a few taels of silver on a birthday gift to celebrate the birthday of the county magistrate's concubine, only to get a meal and a day of running around. Although he later received a reward of "Officer Chen handles affairs diligently," he always felt that this was an unprecedented waste of money in his life.

Mr. Chen likes friends. On the road, even though he wears reading glasses, he always smiles broadly and nods repeatedly. Therefore, some people call him "Jian Shenqu" - seeing people he's crooked. He especially likes visiting friends in restaurants and hotels. In fact, Mr. Chen's alcohol capacity is very small. Four taels of Dushao is enough to make his face red and his ears hot, but his meat capacity is not small. A standard pig's trotter skin can be rolled up and eaten all at once. He always boasts: "I have too many friends. I have to eat and drink for at least five or six years for three meals a day." This is definitely not his boasting. We often see him drunk, oily, and very satisfied wandering on the road.

Mr. Chen is very frugal. He likes simple people, whether he knows them or not, he always politely says hello based on old accounts. But he must personally attend to congratulate or condole. At the table, he always likes to sit at the same table with children. He said: "Children are the most innocent and innocent." He loves to eat pig's trotter skin the most, so he always points his bamboo chopsticks at the pig's trotter and shouts "The trotter wants to be sealed," and then he rolls it up and eats it all at once. So, some people call him "Trotter Sealer".

Mr. Chen has no wife or children. In addition to socializing and drinking, most of his time every day is spent in teahouses, and he is an old tea customer regardless of the size of the teahouse. When he steps into the teahouse, he scans the whole hall with his eyes under his glasses. In his nodding and smiling voice, he will find tea friends. Therefore, some people respectfully call him Patrol - Tea - Censor.

But Mr. Chen sometimes loudly calls out: "I am ultimately ivory soap, and I have encountered an all-pervasive iron scrub brush, which is why I make you feel annoyed"!

Switching Phoenixes

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 8: Swearing Allegiance with a Cup of Water, Talking About Weariness Under a Green Lamp, Red Beans Reporting Longing with Golden Lines

Youmei slowly sat on the chair beside her, propped her head with her hand, lowered her eyelids, thought for a while, and then smiled: Although I have not experienced this kind of situation, I am thinking carefully that if I were you, my mood must be like this, and I can't simply talk about what's in my heart. Because you are much more stable and thorough than me. At this time, you are so overwhelmed that you can't control yourself. Can a careless person like me find a clue? Menglan said: That's your wrong observation. A generous person like you can't be as indecisive as me, so you won't be in such an incurable situation. For yourself, you would have thought of a solution long ago. Youmei was already holding her chin with both hands upward, staring at the roof, and nodding her head: Of course, I am not willing to sacrifice under the old etiquette. However, my family is not much better than yours. Alas! It would be better for us to be born twenty years earlier or twenty years later, but we were born in a transitional era. As if we were endowed with freedom, but we couldn't get free. Menglan did not take up his words, and sighed even more deeply. Just at this time, she heard the stairs ringing, and Menglan shook her hands at Youmei twice. Xiaoju followed outside the door and shouted: Miss, I'm outside the door, am I called or not? I put my fingers in my ears, so I can't hear what you're saying. Youmei said: Xiaoju, are you still plugging your ears now? Xiaoju didn't say anything? Youmei said: Why don't you say anything? This girl is so bold. Xiaoju said: I promised, didn't I hear Li Xia say something without plugging my ears? Youmei said: You are speaking now, did you hear what I said after all? Xiaoju smiled and jumped in, plugging her ears with two index fingers and smiled: Miss Li, look, look, did I plug my ears? Menglan sighed: Xiaoju, your fate is better than mine. You are carefree and don't know anything. We have studied books for more than ten years, and we are not as good as you at all. Xiaoju pursed her mouth and said: That's the world turned upside down, and the lady is not as good as the maid? I know, Miss, you are complaining again. Her hands were already down, not plugging her ears, and pointing at the tip of her nose with her right index finger, and pointing at Youmei with a smile: Miss Li told our madam that she will definitely persuade our miss to change her mind. You told me not to tell you, my miss treats me well, I can't help but tell you. These words made both Mei and Lan laugh endlessly. (99)

The Spirit of Art

— Lang Luxun

Ms. Zhou Minyi has been studying painting for more than twenty years. She left school long ago and is now a housewife in charge, a mother to a child. She can no longer immerse all her energy and time in painting as she did in school. Inevitably, like other women, she is burdened with household chores, the trivialities of family life occupy her, but she does not neglect her art. Amidst her household duties, she continues to work hard at her studies. I have seen how many talented women have been buried in the environment of their families, which always makes me lament their future! Today, Ms. Zhou fundamentally refutes the notion of women's dormitories. Looking at Ms. Zhou's large body of work over the years, it further proves to us that women in families do not necessarily have their talents completely submerged.

The attitude of women pursuing art is that they do not regard art as a pastime but as a career. She has even greater artistic aspirations, spending her days with palette and paintbrush as close friends, day after day for twenty years. Unfortunately, a serious blow came suddenly. The ruthless artillery fire of the "January 28th Incident" burned Ms. Zhou's accumulated drafts almost completely. Even the books and pictures she usually collected were buried in the fire. Unexpectedly, such a major blow not only failed to destroy Ms. Zhou's ambition, but after the "January 28th Incident," she turned adversity into acceptance, reorganized her artistic endeavors, and has been even more diligent in recent years than before. Although the quantity of her paintings is not as much as before, the quality has clearly taken on a new form. Those beautiful lines, gentle and beautiful colors, and deeply touching expressions undoubtedly give me the recognition that they come from the pen of an artist who has been tempered by blows and is even stronger.

This time, Ms. Zhou's friends repeatedly encouraged her to carefully select more than a hundred oil paintings from her works after the "January 28th Incident" and hold a solo exhibition in Shanghai. I am writing these few words specifically as an introduction, hoping that Ms. Zhou will continue her past spirit of pursuing art, redouble her efforts, and make great contributions to the art world in the future, shining like a rare and magnificent comet among the stars.

The Pleasure of Sight and Sound

— Ziwei

Since autumn, there has been no rain, and the chrysanthemums have been severely affected. Even with all the efforts of the Ju Ju family in irrigation, it is still not enough. A few days ago, the heavens finally sent down some timely rain, and the chrysanthemums burst into bloom. Chrysanthemum exhibitions in the Shanghai area are springing up everywhere, too numerous to count. "Guan Nong" in Caojing, West Shanghai, has risen to prominence at the right time, inviting guests to admire the flowers. As I live nearby, I couldn't help but go and take a look.

"Guan Nong" has planted three thousand pots of chrysanthemums. It was also a sensation last year on this day. This time, they have collaborated with the famous "Xiao Guan Yuan," known for its chrysanthemum cultivation, and there are also goldfish on display, making it even grander. Around the "Song Mei" variety, which is entering the competition, are many "Standing Chrysanthemums," with hundreds of flowers on one plant, which is very spectacular. In Wangmei Pavilion, more than ten pots of carefully cultivated fine varieties are arched high, each branch standing tall and gracefully charming. On the walls hang more than twenty pieces of calligraphy and painting by famous masters from the Qing Dynasty, which are truly treasures, from the collection of the famous doctor Qu Zhibu, not marked with prices, entirely for people to enjoy.

On the large lawn in the corner of the bronze lion, chrysanthemums are piled into mountains, and the style is also very beautiful, as tall as the house, making it even more magnificent. The walls of the Green Shade Thatched Cottage are hung with calligraphy and paintings by contemporary artists, such as Zhang Yuguang's Crane, Zhu Dake's inscription, Han Guojun's running script couplet, Jin Liang's ancient seal script couplet, and Qian Shoutie's combined brocade painted screen, all of which are worthy of praise, totaling nearly a hundred pieces, while the rest are mediocre.

A long field is planted with five-colored "Baby's Breath," which is also quite spectacular from a distance. According to Manager Xi, in recent days, many customers who have admired the chrysanthemums have spent money to buy them, with dozens of cases happening every day, and trucks can't deliver them all in time, showing that people who are fascinated by elegance are not saving money despite the economic downturn.

Goldfish are also placed in pots on the grass, with clear and easy-to-read labels, and there are as many as twenty or thirty varieties!

After admiring the chrysanthemums, I was invited by Zhuang Meisheng to a restaurant to eat crabs. Suddenly, on the way, I met Tang Jun Xiumei, and we went to the Empire Theater to appreciate Bai Yushuang's newly staged Ping opera "The West Chamber."

Outside the Pengpeng Theater, friends have often argued about how such-and-such a performer is, but I had never listened to them. Today, after watching Bai's West Chamber, it is not much different from the Peking opera version. I asked Tang, and he said that there was originally no such play in Ping opera, and it was newly adapted from Peking opera. Bai is so charming that it's no wonder so many people are captivated.

In deep autumn, my thoughts are mixed. Stealing half a day of leisure is indeed a great pleasure for the eyes and ears. How can I not record it?

Special Feature

Female Waitresses in Shanghai

— Ying Dai

A friend who strolls around entertainment venues, using their nickname "Glass Cup," talked about the female waitresses of Shanghai. There were indeed some unforgettable and romantic anecdotes in my memory. The first entertainment venue in Shanghai to employ female waitresses was the Paradise World. At that time, the female waitresses of Paradise World were all recruited through examinations. After being selected, they underwent considerable training before being assigned to serve in various tea halls. In terms of appearance, some of the female waitresses in Paradise World were indeed not bad. Dressed in uniform clothing, they served tea to the tourists, shuttling back and forth like weavers. In addition to the female waitresses, the tea managers and cashiers in each tea hall of Paradise World were also young women. Of course, they were relatively knowledgeable and had received considerable education. Later, although it deteriorated year by year, compared to other entertainment venues, the female waitresses of Paradise World were still a cut above the rest!

The Paradise World venue was small and had few recreational activities, but for a period, it caused quite a stir among many tourists, which was due to the appeal of the female waitresses. At that time, in this city of Shanghai, there were many wandering bees and butterflies whose hearts were not in the tea. They went to Paradise World for the female waitresses. There were even many college students who had romantic affairs with female waitresses. If they took a fancy to a female waitress, they would go to drink tea every day. In fact, a cup of tea was only two cents, but they would give a dollar, two dollars, or even five or ten dollars. In this kind of evil environment, many female waitresses were naturally tempted by money. As a result, female waitresses became a kind of woman who sold their bodies, although there were some who were clean and refused to be tempted.

Since the dance craze became popular in Shanghai, it seems that fewer people were interested in female waitresses. Now, with the advent of the economic downturn, the whole of Shanghai has become very depressed, and all industries have been greatly affected. Female waitresses are naturally no exception. The golden age has long passed, and the wealthy who would give one or two dollars for a pot of tea are long gone. Although every entertainment venue still hires female waitresses, it is only as a decoration.

From the First Edition to the Fourth Edition of "Traces of Fragrance"

— Qin Shouou

From the first edition of this book published as a separate volume, it has been less than seven months, and it is actually going to be reprinted for the fourth edition. Many good friends have congratulated me for this, thinking it is a very honorable thing. I won't say any false words; of course, I also feel very gratified. However, in the publishing world at home and abroad, books that go from the first edition to the fourth edition within half a year are not uncommon and are not worth mentioning. Moreover, the statistics show that there are only seven or eight thousand copies, not even reaching ten thousand. Such sales figures are really not enough to be called huge.

To go a step further, because I am the translator of this book, I am naturally the person who knows its contents most clearly. So, if someone asked me, "Do you hope that this book will be published in the fifth and sixth editions?" I would definitely answer, "No, I don't." This is not because I have already sold the copyright of this book to Shenbao, and I have no personal benefit, but because the content of this book, apart from having very delicate and profound descriptions of all people, things, and objects, and being easy to make people laugh, really has no great value. Especially at this critical juncture when the national crisis is deepening day by day, and the survival of the nation is about to be judged in the near future, I think that the reading materials needed by the public should be works full of stimulation and bloodiness, definitely not this kind of thing!

When this book was published in Shenbao on a daily basis, the media and critics had repeatedly commented or corrected it. After the publication of the separate volume, in theory, I should have sent this book to all parties to ask for guidance. However, because I have been very depressed in recent years, closed my doors to guests, and rarely socialized, and I dare not call myself a writer, I have never asked any major writers for advice on this book. For this reason, in the past half year, I have not seen a single gentleman who has given me a complete and satisfactory critique. What I have seen are only two kinds of writing: one is to attack forcefully based on facts, and the other is to casually select a paragraph of facts and reprint it. I think both of these attitudes are wrong. The former is to criticize a novel from the perspective of a historian, which is inevitably too serious, and the latter is to praise a literary work with the means of promoting a celebrity, which is inevitably too excessive. Because the strength of this book is definitely not the truthfulness of narration, so textual research is unnecessary, and reprinting is also meaningless.

Now that the fourth edition is about to be published, I sincerely hope that all the gentlemen or ladies who have already read this book can give me some valuable criticism. (Please send the manuscript to this journal.)

Commentary

The So-Called "Mistakes of Sino-Japanese Negotiations"

— Kawasaki

On the one hand, they use airplanes and cannons to invade our country's territory, and on the other hand, they propose certain conditions to negotiate with us. The deep meaning behind this is obvious.

In the eyes of our neighbors, it seems that the inability to adjust relations between China and Japan is caused by the anti-Japanese movement in China. Therefore, it must be "completely eradicated," even to the point of "resorting to other resolute methods to achieve their goals."

As for why the anti-Japanese movement arose, they believe that "adjusting relations is an extremely difficult task," so they should not bring up the issues of preventing unfortunate incidents and adjusting relations at the same time. Moreover, they are engaging in work with a threatening posture. As a result, the longer the time passes, the more it will incite the anti-Japanese movement. However, they have forgotten that during the negotiations, they bombed Pingdiquan with airplanes and attacked Sui East and Sui North with a large army. Is this what they call "resolute methods"?

It has been a full five years since the September 18th Incident! In these five years, our neighbors have created many unfortunate incidents in our country, such as seizing the five northeastern provinces and eastern Hebei, bombing Shanghai, manipulating North China, and currently using the Datong Line and instigating Mongolian troops to attack Sui province! In the past five years, how many compatriots have been killed, and how much property has been lost? We have not forgotten these, and we are constantly reminded of them by the continuous development of these unfortunate incidents.

Of course, presenting various conditions with a threatening posture will incite the anti-Japanese movement. But will resolutely stopping negotiations on the North China anti-communist problem and other issues that are not directly related to the unfortunate anti-Japanese incidents lead to the discovery of a path to adjustment? The problem is not that simple. To find a path to adjustment, it is naturally necessary to "completely eradicate the anti-Japanese movement." But to completely eradicate the anti-Japanese movement, it is necessary to fundamentally eliminate the various causes that create the anti-Japanese movement. This means that the Japanese authorities should absolutely prohibit any behavior that is likely to cause antipathy from China and revoke all established facts, such as withdrawing troops stationed in China and returning all occupied territories. In this way, the anti-Japanese movement will naturally disappear, and the relations between the two countries will naturally be adjusted, and unfortunate incidents will never happen again. Conversely, if they demand adjustment on the one hand, and on the other hand, use airplanes and cannons to massacre our people and create new unfortunate incidents, then there is no way to adjust relations, and it will only further incite the anti-Japanese movement, which is a great mistake indeed.

In short, if the authorities of our neighboring country do not stop their aggression, then the hope of adjustment is no different from climbing a tree to catch fish.
